* Extremely satisfied
* Somewhat satisfied
* Somewhat unsatisfied
* Extremely unsatisfied
* Not applicable

8. How would you rate the work-life balance in your current job?

* Extremely satisfied
* Somewhat satisfied
* Somewhat unsatisfied
* Extremely unsatisfied
* Not applicable

9. How satisfied are you with the opportunities for growth and learning in your current job?

* Extremely satisfied
* Somewhat satisfied
* Somewhat unsatisfied
* Extremely unsatisfied
* Not applicable

10. On a scale of 1-10, how would you rate the overall job satisfaction?

These questions can be used to gather information about an employee's satisfaction with their workplace, and can be used to identify areas for improvement. The use of a scale of 1-10 and the option of "Not applicable" allows for a more nuanced response, and the multiple choice options give a more concrete understanding of the employee's feelings.

1. Can you tell me about the circumstances that led to the end of your working relationship with the company?

10. Do you have any thoughts or recommendations for the company to improve their processes and prevent similar endings of working relationships in the future?

This is a JSON object that represents a survey about career progression in a company. The survey contains 12 questions (Q1 to Q12) about different aspects of career progression, such as having a clear understanding of career paths, feeling prepared for promotions, and understanding the promotion process. The questions are presented as multiple-choice questions with "Yes" and "No" as options.

The questions are displayed in a specific order, and each question has a unique code that can be used to identify it. The questions are also associated with a type of question, which is indicated by the `TYPE_ID` property. In this case, all questions are of type 1, which means they are multiple-choice questions with a single answer.

The `ANSWERS` property of each question contains a list of objects that represent the answer options. Each object has an `ANSWER` property that contains the text of the answer option.

This survey can be used to assess the level of satisfaction and engagement of employees with their career progression in the company and identify areas for improvement.

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure, I can help you generate a questionnaire on Career Path Clarity. Here are some questions that can be used to gauge how clear employees feel about their career paths within the company:

1. How often do you feel like you have a clear understanding of what steps you need to take to advance in your career within the company?
2. Have you ever felt like you are stuck in a dead-end job with no clear path to something better?
3. Do you feel like you have the same opportunities for advancement as others in the company?
4. How often do you feel like you are able to make informed decisions about your career path based on the information available to you?
5. Do you feel like the company provides you with enough resources and support to help you achieve your career goals?
6. Have you ever felt like you are being held back from achieving your career goals because of the actions or decisions of your supervisors or management?
7. How often do you feel like you have a clear understanding of how your current role fits into the larger organizational structure and how it can help you achieve your career goals?

 Sure, here is a questionnaire on the topic of Career Path Clarity:

1. How clear do you feel about your current career path?

3. Have you ever felt like you were on a "dead-end" job or career path?
4. How often do you evaluate and reassess your career goals and path?

10. How often do you feel like you are learning and growing in your current role?
11. Have you ever felt like you were not being given the opportunity to learn new skills in your current role?
12. How often do you feel like you are able to use your skills and abilities to their fullest extent in your current role?
13. How often do you feel like you are able to contribute to the goals and objectives of your company?
14. Have you ever felt like you were not being recognized for your contributions to your current role?
15. How often do you feel like you are able to make a meaningful impact on your company and its goals?
16. Have you ever felt like you were not being given the resources or support you needed to be successful in your role?
17. How often do you feel like you are able to make a difference in your current role?
18. Have you ever felt like you were not being given the opportunity to work on projects that were meaningful to you?
19. How often do you feel like you are able to work on projects that are challenging and interesting to you?
20. Have you ever felt like you were not being given the opportunity to work with a diverse group of people in your current role?
21. How often do you feel like you are able to work with a diverse group of people in your current role?
22. Have you ever felt like you were not being given the opportunity to work in a supportive and collaborative environment?
23. How often do you feel like you are able to work in a supportive and collaborative environment in your current role?
24. Have you ever felt like you were not being given the opportunity to work in a positive and respectful environment?
25. How often do you feel like you are able to work in a positive and respectful environment in your current role?

| Question | Answer Choices |
| --- | --- |

| Do you feel like there are clear opportunities for advancement in your current role? | Yes, No |

Generate me a questionnaire on Internal Mobility Opportunities

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure, I can help you with that! Here is a questionnaire on Internal Mobility Opportunities:

1. How would you describe the current internal mobility opportunities within the company?
2. Have you personally been given the chance to work in different departments or on various projects?
3. In your opinion, how important is it for an employee to have the opportunity to work in different areas of the company?
4. Does the company provide enough resources and support for employees who want to switch to a different role or department?
5. How does the company help employees to prepare for a new role or position?
6. In your experience, how easy or difficult is it for an employee to move to a different position within the company?
7. Can you name any initiatives or programs that the company has implemented to encourage internal mobility?
8. How does the company measure the success of internal mobility?
9. In your opinion, what are the benefits and drawbacks of internal mobility?
10. Does the company provide enough training and development opportunities for employees who want to advance in their careers?

And here is the questionnaire in a more conversational format:

1. Can you tell me a little bit about the internal mobility opportunities within the company? Are there many chances to work in different departments or on various projects?
2. Have you personally been able to work in different areas of the company or on different projects? If yes, could you share your experience?
3. In your opinion, how crucial is it for an employee to have the opportunity to work in different areas of the company?
4. Does the company provide enough resources and support for employees who want to switch to a different role or department? If not, what could be improved?

1. How often do you feel pressured to meet certain targets or deadlines at work?
2. Do you feel that you have enough resources and support to complete your tasks, or do you often feel like you are "stretched thin"?
3. Have you ever felt pressure to work longer hours or on weekends to meet certain goals?
4. Do you feel that the expectations and goals set for you are reasonable, or do you feel like they are unrealistic?
5. Have you ever felt pressure to hide your mistakes or shortcomings in order to appear more competent?
6. Do you feel that you are able to speak up and share your concerns if you are feeling pressured, or do you feel like you have to keep quiet to avoid confrontation?
7. Have you ever felt pressure to conform to certain norms or expectations in order to fit in with your team?
8. Do you feel that you have the freedom to take time off when you need it, or do you feel like you have to push through and work while sick?
9. Have you ever felt pressure to prioritize certain tasks over others, even if it means sacrificing quality?
10. Do you feel that the pressure you experience at work is due to external factors, such as a heavy workload, or internal factors, such as personality traits or personal expectations?

To convert this questionnaire into a specified format, please let me know which format you would like it to be in. I can convert it into a Microsoft Word document, a Google Doc, a PDF, or even a physical printed copy if needed!

7. How can we improve our recognition and rewards system to make employees feel more valued? Or is it just about the right rewards?
8. Do you think that recognition and rewards are effective in motivating employees to perform better? Or do you think that people are motivated by something deeper?
9. Have you ever faced any challenges in receiving recognition and rewards for your work? Or do you feel that it's always smooth sailing?
10. How does it make you feel when you are recognized and rewarded for your work? Does it give you a sense of accomplishment or just a little bump in your bank account?

This is a JSON object that represents a questionnaire about training and development programs. The questionnaire has five questions, and each question has a code, name, type, and a set of possible answers. Here is a brief explanation of each question:

* `Q1`: Whether the training and development programs are easily accessible to all employees. The possible answers range from strongly agree to strongly disagree.
* `Q2`: The relevance of the training and development programs to the employee's job and the overall goals of the company. The possible answers are given on a scale from 1 to 10.
* `Q3`: The employee's ability to apply the skills and knowledge gained from the training and development programs to their work. The possible answers are given on a scale from 1 to 10.
* `Q4`: The quality of the training and development programs. The possible answers are given on a scale from 1 to 10.
* `Q5`: The factors that determine the employee's decision to participate or not in training and development programs. The possible answers are a list of factors such as learning new skills, cost, and pressure from supervisors.

The `TYPE_ID` property is used to determine the type of question. In this case, all questions are of type 3, which means they are rated on a scale. The `DISPLAY_ORDER` property is used to order the questions in a meaningful way.

Here is a code snippet that can be used to parse and display the questionnaire:

```javascript
const questionnaire = {
  // ...
};

function displayQuestionnaire(questionnaire) {
  for (const question of questionnaire._TF_QUESTIONS) {
    console.log(question.NAME);
    console.log("Possible answers:");
    for (const answer of question._TF_ANSWERS) {
      console.log(answer.ANSWER);
    }
    console.log("----------------------------------");
  }
}

displayQuestionnaire(questionnaire);
```

     - Question number: 8

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on WorkLife Balance

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure, I can help you generate a questionnaire on WorkLife Balance. Here is a set of questions that can be used to gauge the work-life balance of employees:

1. How many hours do you work per week, including overtime?
2. Do you feel like you have enough time to do your job effectively?
3. How often do you feel exhausted or stressed because of work?
4. How often do you bring work home with you, either physically or mentally?
5. How often do you feel like you have to choose between work and personal life?
6. How often do you take time off when you are eligible?
7. How often do you feel like your personal life is being neglected due to work?
8. Do you feel that your work is valued and respected within the company?
9. Do you have the resources and support you need to do your job effectively?
10. How often do you feel like you are able to balance your work and personal life?
11. How often do you feel that your personal life is being intruded upon by work?
12. Do you feel that the company's policies and practices promote a healthy work-life balance?

 Sure, I can help you generate a questionnaire on Workload Management. Here are some questions that can be used to gather information about how an organization manages workload and whether the right balance is being maintained:

1. How does the organization determine the workload capacity for each team or department?
2. What tools and techniques are used to manage workload and ensure that it is evenly distributed?
3. Does the organization have a process in place to monitor workload and adjust it as needed? If so, what are the key components of this process?
4. How are employees involved in the workload management process, and what role do they play in maintaining a healthy work-life balance?
5. Does the organization have a clear definition of what constitutes a "heavy" workload, and if so, what is it?
6. How are priorities set when it comes to workload management, and how are less critical tasks handled?
7. What steps are taken to ensure that workload is managed in a way that is both efficient and sustainable?
8. Does the organization have a process in place to identify and mitigate burnout, and if so, what are the key components of this process?
9. How does the organization handle workload fluctuations, such as during peak times or during absences of team members?
10. Does the organization have a process in place to ensure that workload is managed in a way that is both fair and equitable?
11. How does the organization communicate about workload management, and what role does communication play in maintaining a healthy work-life balance?
12. Does the organization have a process in place to measure the impact of workload management on employee satisfaction and productivity?

[LLM ANSWER]

1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere of the workplace? Is it generally positive and collaborative, or does it feel tense and hostile?
2. Have you ever felt unsafe or uncomfortable in your workplace? If so, what steps were taken to address the issue?
3. How would you rate the level of cleanliness and organization in your workplace? Do you think it affects your productivity and focus?
4. Are there any specific elements of the workplace environment, such as lighting, temperature, or noise level, that you feel could be improved?
5. How often do you interact with your colleagues and how would you rate the quality of those interactions?
6. Do you feel that the physical space of the workplace is conducive to creativity and innovation?
7. Have you ever felt that your personal identity is being compromised by the workplace environment?
8. How well do you feel that the workplace environment supports your health and well-being?
9. Do you feel that the physical space of the workplace is accessible and inclusive to all employees?
10. How often do you have to work from home or other places and how does it affect your productivity and focus?

Please let me know if you would like me to convert this questionnaire into a specific format!
